[Brh_1,7. bhuktiḥ]
[Brh_1,7.]
dhanamūlāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā $ yatnās tatsādhane matāḥ &

[Brh_1,7.1 dhanaprabhedāḥ]

yathāvidhena dravyeṇa $ yat kiñ cit kurute naraḥ &

tat punar dvādaśavidhaṃ $ prativarṇāśrayaṃ smṛtam &

[Brh_1,11.3 sthāpana-prakāraḥ]
